323b3(kha): 'jzugs bskun dang // pe gzhi legs bgrigs byas pa'i 'grels yel yengs khyab byed srel dad zen na'ang / g.sung dung ben gyi dpe gzhi' bsdu bgrigs byed pa'io ga rkabs kyi thed sdug de tsam byung 
323b4(kha): med pas/ 'di'i phyegs la nyams myeng dang lag len segs la lig zhes len gzhi dken pas gol cha gsad du yin pa dang / sghes su de zhus bgrigs pa che yang mkhyen dbyed dab 'byams pa min 
323b5(kha): thad/ 'di' thad mthun rkyen zung la 'gal rkyen mang ba'i gseb ru dal brling 'grig pa dang ma byung na/ phyegs gang sa'i thed ypug dang gnas sdangs tsha las brgal ba'i legs cha zhig then thabs 
323b6(kha): med pas/ de lugs kyis rjes su gzigs mkhan rnam pas 'di la dg rkyen thad ye bsrang yong nges gnang de che zhing / 'di yi byas pa 'dis kyang sad du g.yung dung ban gyi lung gi bstan pa den po che gsal / 
324a1(kha): hyo/ dg khroga' nam tsho' bram bhogsho rnacmad had namci bca/ bang nan / a/ 
324a2(kha): blang g a tbrul lo'g ba / chos bnyan/ rmyola 2a nyan// 
324a3(kha): byung po nang cen dgon go lr dpe zhas chan pas// 
324a4(kha): ceods'o/
